<Review>I will begin by saying that these are my honest observations while attending Spartan from Nov 2019 through July 2021 (through Covid).  This may be long, but you will find it insightful and honest.
The facilities.  Like most everyone else, I was impressed when I took the tour before I enrolled.  A lot of equipment in two separate hangers looked great.  But after I enrolled and took all the classes, I know better.  There isn't one piece of aircraft equipment that is presently working or isn't missing any parts.  Manuals are disorganized or missing pages.  It is an old school built in the mid 1940's and it shows. The buildings need updating as does the equipment.  I can say that the administration is working on updating the facilities, but it will take a long time to bring them up to date.  Despite the facilities and equipment, it is still possible to learn the necessary knowledge you need to get your A&P license.  This is largely due to a dedicated faculty staff that has gone out of their way to ensure that I get the knowledge I need.
The faculty.  One of the best teachers I've ever had in any classroom setting is Mr Gober.  While he is not a licensed A&P mechanic, his math lessons are entertaining and to the point. The faculty is full of knowledgeable and experienced individuals that are trying to make a difference in your life, despite what is going on around them. I thank Mr Gober, Mr Miller, Mr Rapp, Mr Post, Dr. Boyce, Mr Harrell, Mr Freed, Mr Apollonio, Mr Anderson, Mr Chojnicki, Mr Jordan and Mr Douglas for taking the time and extra effort to make sure that I understood every aspect of the topic being taught.  They are a wealth of information and anyone that tells you different, has not taken the time to ask questions or speak with them individually. They all have different teaching styles, and some may not like the style, but they are effective if the student puts forth the effort.  THE FACULTY FULLY DESERVE A 5 STAR RATING.
Some students attend school, show up prepared, put forth the effort and complete their work in a timely manner.  Others just show up and go through the motions.  Yes, I paid a substantial amount of money to get the education, but I also worked hard to achieve my educational goals. When possible, I showed up early, stayed late and asked questions.  Unfortunately, I can't say the same about some other students.
If you have a concern or if you want something done, then you go to Linda Laim.  She is the Dean of Student Affairs and has been a tremendous help to me and most other students. If you ask anyone on campus who they call when they need help, they will more than likely say "Linda" another 5 STAR RATING recipient.  In my time at Spartan, we have gone through three campus presidents.  The first left after the first month I was there, so I did not get to know him.  The second always had time to listen to the students but follow up was limited.  Whether it was because of Covid restrictions, a lack of accountability, or lack of support from corporate is anyone's guess, but the fact remains that there was limited follow up and/or execution that I was able to discern. The current campus president I don't know much about since he's been here about 2 months.  This is his second tour with the school and I am hoping that he can get this school to what we all envision it to be.
Would I recommend the school?  It depends.  If you are a self motivated, willing to do what needs to be done regardless of the situation, then yes.  But if you are anything else, this may not be the school for you as you will feel like most others who have given the school a bad review. I can tell you that I completed the curriculum and I'm looking forward to testing for my A&P.  I am still continuously encouraged and helped by the faculty and administration so that I can achieve that goal.
The school is old and has its problems.  But the school also has a lot of potential (and it is slowly getting better). The school will be what you make of it.<//Review>< pictures>
None</pictures>

< Text>
I feel like I really want to leave this review not only as a former student/graduate, not only as a former employee of SkyWest Airlines, not only as a former instructor for Spartan but as current Dean of Academic Affairs for Spartan. I was an automotive mechanic and knew that I wanted to do something more and came to this school. I heard the same complaints that I have read, but noticed something about the people who were the loudest. I noticed I don't see many of those people in the industry today. The former students I see in the industry, I have seen at SkyWest, at Qantas Airlines, at Space X and Delta Airlines. I also see them in General Aviation repair stations and in many of the manufacturing facilities, (Northrop Grumman, Robinson,  Panasonic etc.) The school's goal is to help you get the Airframe/Powerplant Certification. The equipment that we have is equipment that the exams, given by the FAA, specifically ask about. We will touch on the electric braking systems on current 787s but that won't be on the exams and we have to walk a fine line in between what we want to tell you about the current industry and the data saturation point when taking your exams. We are very proud of our instructors. If you take the total number of time in the industry of all of our instructors myself included, is nearly 250 years of experience. We know what it takes to get into the industry and are very proud of the students that come back and talk at our alumni panels. We're very proud of the reputation of the number of people that take the written exams and pass which would surpass in three months what the local schools will put out in 2 years. (Google NORMS 8080-08).  The aircraft industry needs more than a few good mechanics. You can't get something for nothing. We train mechanics that want to be mechanics. We are Spartan.<//Text>

< review>
Great instructors. Most people pay around 25k with financial aid. However just beware everything you see in these pictures is bullshit. You will not get to work on anything you think. all parts are old 1960 carburators, magnetos and engines. the planes are half ass cessna 150's. when it comes to hands on be ready to "use your imagination" because everything on the inglewood campus either doesnt work or is missing parts or is out dated.
If youre serious, i mean SERIOUS about your A&P this school is no problem but if youre counting on this school as a career launch pad and teaching you the latest and greatest, save your money and try out the industry first to be sure this is what you want.
Theres plenty of companies out there willing to hire non A&Ps to get your feet wet.</review>

< text>
On Yelp there were many 5 star reviews but after eating and looked at more recent there are a lot of 1-3 star ones. Here's the reason why, the rolls are simply too big some might say that's more food but when eating sushi the rolls should be bite size and not you chocking if you attempt to eat these monstrous rolls. A pro I would say is that the food came out in less than 10 minutes of ordering. The fish for the sushi was 7/10 for freshness taste, but I did not enjoy the added topping that came on the sushi, it's suppose to bring out the fish flavour not overpower it. They have quite a selection for sushi so if you feel like trying something new they got you covered. Ordered 2 rolls, 3 different types of sushi fish, 1 hand roll, and tempura, usually for this amount of food we pay 50-60 but the total was 70, very expensive for sub par sushi. If you want to satisfy you sushi craving this is an okay choice but not the best especially for the price.</text>

< Text>
This is my favorite place to eat. Suitable for any mood. I tend to go most often when im feeling or overwhelmed. The atmosphere is so cozy. Its one of the only places I get hot tea at. It just feels right. I've kinda of fallen in love with this place. The staff, the food. Never a bad experience. It's just nice and uplifting to eat there. The staff is very tentative and friendly. One time I even had one of the chefs give me a little extra eel after I only had rice left to my unagidon. The food and presentation are definitely evolving to a more fancy appeal. It looks a lot better presented than it used to be but the flavor is still as amazing as it was back then. Honestly for me tho it isn't about the fancy platters and stuff. I really love the cozy homely vibe. Almost feels safe there. I can just truly relax. Can be a bit pricey depending on what ur going for but I think its worth it. For the atmosphere,  service, and food.< /Text>

< name>
Adeline Churlburt</name>
<Time>1568828969234< /Time><Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
Kazama Sushi, thank you for bringing delicious Japanese food to the Claremont area! I have been a frequent visitor since moving into the Claremont area and have been consistently satisfied by the service, food and affordability of this restaurant.

The portion sizes are generous for everything I've tried. This includes various rolls, the bento box sets, tempura lunch set, and tempura udon. I'm personally a fan of their speciality rolls because of how much flavor and seafood stuffed into each piece. Their tempura is also as good as any other good Japanese restaurant, having a variety of vegetables and shrimp.

Another plus of Kazama is their all-day sake bomb special for $1.99 each. For anyone new to the sake bomb scene, this is a $1.99 combo of beer and sake shot. It's not only tasty but leaves you feeling a little extra happy during your meal time.

Conclusion? One of the best and affordable Japanese restaurants in the area.< /Review>

Super attentive staff!
Even though i don't necessary enjoyed my roll, i still gave it 4 star for the great customer service!

My poo and I decided to get sushi and walked through the back and was immediately seated. The lady noticed the table was moving ( i didn't even noticed) and she quickly fixed it. We decided to start off with sake bombs for $2 each and even though it was just the two of us it was soo fun!

My favorite was the fried tofu steak, i could of just ate that instead of my rolls. For some reason it had this odd after taste!

My man also felt his sushi was subpar but once again the attentiveness was undeniable ...so really this place deserve a 3.5 star overall.<//Text>

(Translated by Google) You can eat authentic sushi at a store run by a Japanese person, which is rare in the area.
Not only the standard sushi, but also sashimi, grilled fish (salted yellowtail if you remember correctly), miso soup, and beer were all eaten with the same taste as you would normally eat in Japan.
Also, I ate California roll for the first time, which I can't eat at Japanese sushi restaurants, but it was delicious.
By the way, I was able to order in Japanese normally because the shop owner responded. I remember that the shop owner was a friendly person and the correspondence was very good.
I stayed there for only 3 weeks, but when I was tired of eating only American food, I was very happy to be able to enjoy the taste of Japan.
* Information when visiting in 2012.

< Review>
The ice cream flavors are good. I‚Äôm a big fan of matcha so I need to try out this place right away when I knew about it. If you cant choose between their matcha and sesame signature ice creams, it would be a great idea to have a combined swirl. They provide spoon to help with scooping the ice cream from the cone. A water station is also provided with lemon ice water. The seating area outside is very cute and the lighting makes it even cuter at night.

Highlights of the menu:
1. Matcha ice cream

<review>As matcha lover, this is one of the best places I would recommend.
The flavor is absolutely RIGHT üòä It is not too sweet or artificial. I have ordered the soft served matcha with sesame  duo. The texture is smooth and milky. The two flavors blend very well. Located in the back of a local Garden Grove bar/arcade called ‚ÄúBarcode,‚Äù Mr. Matcha is Matcha do about softserve.

Sorry about the corny joke, but they play up the puns here ‚Äî e.g. sign that says ‚ÄúHow Matcha do you love me.‚Äù They don‚Äôt mind IGers and even post photo-taking tips.

Most of the seating is in the outdoor patio facing the large parking lot in back of Main Street.

I had a Matcha green tea/black sesame swirl soft serve on a black cone for $4.95 before optional tip. The softserve tasted good, but slightly icy. The black cone is more of a novelty if you ask me and I didn‚Äôt care for the cinnamon notes in the cone ‚Äî I‚Äôm going to skip the cone if I revisit.

Free parking and they have a water station and restroom.< /review>

<userid>103221479260987056557< /userid>< name>
Lynda Nguyen<//name>
<date>1538368409556<//date><rating>5<//rating>< Review>
I've been here 2 days in a row! Cool organic soft serve joint behind a bar. I love matcha & sesame so I had to try them plain & came back the next day to swirl it!

Matcha Green Tea soft serve on day one lived up to my expectations. You can't go wrong with matcha. It's not too sweet & hits the spot if you want to taste the cream of your ice cream & matcha powder from your green tea.

Sesame Soft Serve tastes just like my favorite hot sesame dessert but this one happens to be cold in a cone! It's nutty & gritty just the way I like my black sesame! It's a bit on the sweeter side so if you don't like sweet then order a swirl to balance.

Matcha & Sesame swirl is the perfect combination of milky cream, nutty sesame & matcha. It plays different textures & flavors on your pallet & then mixes nicely together to get that unique taste that's less sweet because the matcha down plays the sesame.

My black cone was perfect on day 1 but it was stale on day 2. I don't understand why but my besties & I were all disappointed on day 2 because it ruined the mood as we got to the cone!

UPDATED TO 5 STARS ON 8/26/17: My son saw my foodie post on my IG so he asked to go try the Black Cone here. Their wish is my command! I would never tell people how I feel because I want them to experience it first hand with their true feelings & own judgement!

The Black Cones were perfect today! But best of all was that my baby girl just asked for a little cup to taste her sibling's Matcha Ice Cream. The server felt bad so he gave my daughter a full cup for free. I didn't expect anything for free but this really made my 7 year old daughter feel special because it's going to be her 8th birthday soon!

Mr. Matcha has the best soft serve & services because the best employees are always happy & cheerful! They never fail to ask me how my day was going!< /Review>

<Review>It was fine.

They were out of cones on a Monday, and their fence out front is broken (probably from a car backing up into it).

The cup price was $5.12 with tax.

They are located in the back of a bar, but you aren't allowed to walk between the two by a sign to the effect of "not an entrance. Please walk around the side of the building and sign in." I think it was attached to a "wet floor" sign, or something similarly sized.

Only come here if you really want a matcha or black sesame ice cream, but there are other places you could probably go to instead.

I hear that a SomiSomi is opening in Garden Grove soon. SomiSomi has comparable flavor quality in their matcha and black sesame, but they aren't going to run out of their gimic ice cream holder on a Monday night.

Seriously, if you run out of cones at an ice cream place, that just goes to show how little you care about your business.

It's just... fine.

Do you want to spend over $5 on fine?< /Review><Pics>None<//Pics>< resp>

< Review>
TL:DR - Matcha ice cream with black sesame cone is the way to go. Matcha latte float is a waste of money.

Went in and ordered two things, the matcha latte float and the matcha ice cream with the black sesame cone.

Matcha ice cream: definitely the thing worth coming here for. Got the traditional green matcha, brimming with flavor and tasting of actual matcha as opposed to the gritty, powdered flavor you can find elsewhere. Nice soft texture, served at the right temperature that went well with the black sesame cone. The come itself held up during the entire treat, not becoming overly soggy throughout the experience. 5/5

Matcha latte float: extremely disappointing. Tasted like I was just drinking milk. Tried mixing the matcha ice cream into the latte to try and save it, mixing the rich flavorful ice cream with the dull, tasteless latte, but to no avail. I ditched the latte halfway through and begged my girlfriend to share her ice cream with me. Waste of your money. 1/5</Review>

Today is my favorite! They changed the code w/o informing me. I had to go to the office to get it, which wasn't easy because i didn't had the code to get out of the gate.
There was not even a chance that lady was going to move from her chair to bring the new code to me. Great Customer  Service Public Storage!
I will move out of there before my stuff is stolen (happen to my storage neighbor today) or the price is going through the roof.

I hope you guys get more competition so you have to work for the $$$ you are getting from us customers!<//review>
